class Solution { public ListNode addTwoNumbers(ListNode l1, ListNode l2) { if (l1 == null) { l1 = new ListNode(0); } if (l2 == null) { l2 = new ListNode(0); } int x = l1.val + l2.val; ListNode r = new ListNode(x % 10); if (l1.next != null || l2.next != null) { if (x >= 10) { if (l1.next != null) { l1.next.val += 1; } else { l2.next.val += 1; } } r.next = addTwoNumbers(l1.next, l2.next); } else { if
